532-8877</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:14pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">NIKE, INC. REPORTS FISCAL </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">FOURTH QUARTER</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:14pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">AND FULL YEAR RESULTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">BEAVERTON, Ore., June 27, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;- NIKE, Inc. (NYSE:NKE) today reported financial results for its fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">fourth quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;and full year ended </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">May&#160;31, 2019</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Fourth quarter revenue increased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$10.2 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">4 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a reported basis and up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">10 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a currency-neutral basis*. Full year revenue rose to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$39.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">7 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a reported basis and up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">11 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a currency-neutral basis, as strategic investments in innovation and digital drove global consumer demand led by NIKE Direct in both periods.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;FY19 was a pivotal year for NIKE as we continue to bring our Consumer Direct Offense to life throughout the marketplace,&#8221; said Mark Parker, Chairman, President and CEO, NIKE, Inc. &#8220;Our distinctive innovation and digital advantage led to accelerated growth across our complete portfolio, while our Brand fueled deeper relationships with consumers around the globe.&#8221;**</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Diluted earnings per share in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">fourth quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$0.62</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;driven by revenue growth, strong gross margin expansion, and a lower average share count, partially offset by higher selling and administrative expense and a higher tax rate. Diluted earnings per share for the full year was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.49</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Reflecting on our FY19 performance, it is clear that growth is paramount at NIKE, and that our strong growth is being driven by strategic transformation,&#8221; said Andy Campion, Executive Vice President and CFO, NIKE, Inc. &#8220;Amid foreign exchange volatility, our double-digit currency-neutral revenue growth and expanding ROIC showcase NIKE&#8217;s unrivaled ability to create extraordinary value for consumers and shareholders over the long term.&#8221;**</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Fourth Quarter</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Income Statement Review</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Revenues</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">for NIKE, Inc. increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">4 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$10.2 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">10 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a currency-neutral basis.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9702;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Revenues for the NIKE Brand were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$9.7 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">10 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a currency-neutral basis, driven by growth across NIKE Direct and wholesale, key categories including Sportswear, Jordan and Basketball, and continued growth across footwear and apparel.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9702;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Revenues for Converse were $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">491 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, flat to prior year on a currency-neutral basis, mainly driven by double-digit growth in Asia and digital which was offset by declines in the U.S. and Europe. </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Gross margin</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">80 basis points</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">45.5 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;due primarily to higher average selling prices, impacts from foreign currency, and growth in NIKE Direct. These benefits were partially offset by higher product costs and supply chain investments. </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Selling and administrative expense</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">9 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$3.4 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. Demand creation expense was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$1.0 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">3 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to prior year due to global brand campaigns and key sports moments. Operating overhead expense increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">12 percent</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$2.4 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;driven primarily by wage-related and administrative expenses, which reflect critical investments in innovation, data and analytics, and new capabilities to accelerate our end-to-end digital transformation. </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; Wholly-owned NIKE, Inc. subsidiary brands include Converse, which designs, markets and distributes athletic lifestyle footwear, apparel and accessories; and Hurley, which designs, markets and distributes surf and youth lifestyle footwear, apparel and accessories.
